**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.24 \|\|**

**śarair agny-arka-saṁsparśair āśī-viṣa-durāsadaiḥ \|**

**pīḍyamāna-purānīkaḥ śālvo'muhyat pareritaiḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : agnivad** dāhakaḥ, **arkavad**
yugapat sarvataḥ **saṁsparśo** yeṣāṁ taiḥ \| **āśī-viṣa**vad
eka-deśa-sparśa-mātreṇa mārakatvād **durāsadair** duḥsahaiḥ
**pīḍyamānaṁ** **puram anīkāni** ca yasya saḥ \| **parair** yadubhir
**īritair** muktaiḥ \|\|24\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : arko**\'rka-raśmiḥ, sa
yathā sarvān apy ekadaiva **samyak spṛśati**, tadvad ity arthaḥ \| anyat
tair vyākhyātam \| tatra sarvata iti sarveṣv ity arthaḥ \|\|24\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : agnayaḥ** dāhakatayā
tad-rūpatvena rūpitā ity arthaḥ \| **arka-saṁsparśā** arkasyeva
raśmi-dvārā sarvatra **saṁsparśas** tāpamayo yeṣāṁ te ca te ca taiḥ
\|\|24\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : agny-arkayor** iva
**sparśo** yeṣāṁ, taiḥ **āśī-viṣaiḥ** sarpair iva **durāsadaiḥ**
duḥsahaiḥ **pīḍyamānaṁ** **puram anīkāni** ca yasya, saḥ \| **parair**
yadubhir **īritair** muktaiḥ \|\|24-25\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.25 \|\|**

**śālvānīkapa-śastraughair vṛṣṇi-vīrā bhṛśārditāḥ \|**

**na tatyajū raṇaṁ svaṁ svaṁ loka-dvaya-jigīṣavaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : bhṛśārditā** api **svaṁ svaṁ
raṇaṁ** svāṁ yuddha-bhūmim \|\|25\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : loka-dvayasya jigīṣavaḥ**
kṣātra-dharma-pravartanārthaṁ yaśo-dharmādy-apekṣakāḥ santaḥ \| yad vā,
jagad-dhitārthaṁ nija-kīrti-vistāraṇena
ūrdhvādho-loka-dvaya-vaśīkaraṇecchava ity arthaḥ \|\|25\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : loka-dvayasya jigīṣavaḥ**
kṣātra-dharma-pravartanārthaṁ yaśo-dharma-pravartanārthaṁ
yaśo-dharmādy-apekṣakāḥ santaḥ \| yad vā, jagad-dhitārthaṁ
nija-kīrti-vistāreṇordhvādho-loka-dvaya-vaśīkaraṇecchava ity arthaḥ
\|\|25\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ),
viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.26 \|\|**

**śālvāmātyo dyumān nāma pradyumnaṁ**[^15] **prāk prapīḍitaḥ \|**

**āsādya gadayā maurvyā vyāhatya vyanadad balī \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : maurvyā** kārṣṇāyasa-mayyā \|
**vyāhatya** prahṛtya \|\|26\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : pradyumnāt prāk**
prakarṣeṇa **pīḍito**\'stra-prahāreṇa duḥkhitaḥ \| \"pradyumnam\" iti
pāṭhe pāṭhānte pradyumnam āsādyety anvayaḥ \| prāk prapīḍitas tenaiva
viśeṣeṇa **āhatya** prahṛtya **vyanadat** atyuccair nādam akarot, yato
**balī** \|\|26\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** pradyumnād dhetoḥ **prāk**
prakarṣeṇa **pīḍitaḥ** astra-prahāreṇa duḥkhitaḥ **vi**śeṣeṇa **āhatya**
prahṛtya \|\|26\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : pradyumnād** dhetoḥ
**prāk** prathamaṁ **pīḍitaḥ** pradyumna-prayuktena astreṇa bādhitaḥ
**maurvyā** kārṣṇāyasa-mayā \|\|26\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.27 \|\|**

**pradyumnaṁ gadayāśīrṇa-vakṣaḥ-sthalam arindamam \|**

**apovāha raṇāt sūto dharma-vid dārukātmajaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : apovāha** anyato nināya \|\|27\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : aśīrṇa-vakṣaḥ-sthalam** apy
**apovāha** \| kim-artham? **arindamaṁ** kṣaṇaṁ viśramya svasthatayā
nijāriṁ damayitum ity arthaḥ \| nanu tathāpi raṇād apavahanam ayuktam ?
tatrāha---**dharmavit**, asvasthasya sato rathino\'vekṣaṇaṁ sārathiḥ
kuryād iti dharmaṁ jānan \| yato **dārukaḥ** śrī-bhagavat-sārathiḥ,
tasya **ātmajaḥ** \|\|27\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : aśīrṇa-vakṣaḥ-sthalam** apy
**apovāha** \| kim-artham **arindamaṁ** kṣaṇaṁ viśramya nijāriṁ
damayitum ity arthaḥ \| tathāpi raṇād apavāhanam ayuktaṁ,
tatrāha---**dharmavit** sārathiḥ rathi-rakṣaṇa-dharmaṁ jānan yato
**dārukasya** **ātmajaḥ** \|\|27\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : taṁ** pradyumna
śīrṇa-vakṣaḥ-sthalam iti prakṛtyā dyumato **gadayā**
cid-ānanda-maya-vakṣasas tasya śīrṇatvāsambhave\'pi līlā-śaktyaiva tam
yuddhotsāha-rasa-vardhanārtham āvega-mātre utpādite, taṁ **gadayaiva**
śīrṇa-vakṣaḥ-sthalaṁ matvā **apovāha** anyatra nināya, yato
**dharmavit** sūtaḥ kṛcchra-gataṁ rakṣet iti dharmajñaḥ, vastutas tu
a-kāra-praśleṣeṇa sac-cid-ānanda-vigrahatva-lakṣaṇaṁ tasya dharmaṁ na
vettīty adharmavit, tac ca tad-ajñānaṁ tam parama-susaṅgatam eva, yato
**dārukātmajaḥ**, parīkṣiti bhaved rāgo dāruke ca tathoddhave
\[bha.ra.si. 3.2.90\] iti bhakti-rasāmṛtokter mahā-premavato
dārukasyātmajaḥ pradyumna-viṣayaka-mahā-snehavān iti bhāvaḥ \|\|27\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.28 \|\|**

**labdha-saṁjño muhūrtena kārṣṇiḥ sārathim abravīt \|**

**aho asādhv idaṁ sūta yad raṇān me'pasarpaṇam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : apasarpaṇaṁ** bahir
nirgamanam \|\|28\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : kārṣṇiḥ**
līlā-kautukākṛṣṭa-cittasya bhagavataḥ putra iti tasyāpi tādṛśatvaṁ
sūcitam \| ato vaicitryādikaṁ sarvaṁ tasya saṅgacchetaiveti bhāvaḥ \|
yad vā, **labdhā saṁjñā** vīreṣu khyātir yena saḥ, ato **muhūrtena**
svasthaḥ sann **abravīd** ity arthaḥ \| **aho** khede, **me**
śrī-yādavendra-putrasya mama \|\|28\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : kārṣṇiḥ** tad-apatyatvena
tadval līlā-vaicitryākṛṣṭa-citta ity arthaḥ \| ato mohādy-anukaraṇaṁ
sarvaṁ saṅgacchetaiveti bhāvaḥ \| **aho** khede **me** mama
śrī-yādavendra-sutasyety arthaḥ \|\|28\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tataś ca **labdhā**
**samyak jñā,** \"anena yuddha-sthalād aham apasāritaḥ\" iti jñānaṁ yena
saḥ kṛtāvadhāna ity arthaḥ \| yad vā, **labdhā saṁjñā** artha-sūcanā
apasāraṇa-vyāpāreṇa sva-mūrchā-jñāpanā sūta-kṛtā yena saḥ \| ata eva taṁ
prati kupitaḥ sann **abravīt**---**asādhv** iti saṁjñā syāc cetanānām
ahastād yaiḥ svārtha-sūcanā ity amaraḥ \| **muhūrtena** kṣaṇena
\|\|28\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.29 \|\|**

**na yadūnāṁ kule jātaḥ śrūyate raṇa-vicyutaḥ \|**

**vinā mat klība-cittena sūtena prāpta-kilbiṣāt**[^16] **\|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : mat** matto **vinā**, **klībaṁ
cittaṁ** yasya tena \| **tvayā** sūtena \|\|29\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : prāptaṁ kalmaṣam** apavādo
yena, tasmāt \| kalmaṣaṁ pāpa-nindayoḥ iti nighaṇṭuḥ \|
\"kilbiṣa\"-pāṭhe\'pi sa evārthaḥ \|\|29\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : raṇād vicyuto**\'pasṛtaḥ
ko\'pi na śrūyate \| **klībaṁ** pauruṣa-hīnaṁ **cittaṁ** yasya tena \|
**sutena** tvayā hetunā **prāptaṁ kilbiṣaṁ** pāpaṁ yena \| yad vā,
prāptaṁ kilbiṣam aparādho yaṁ tasmāt \|\|29\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : klībaṁ** pauruṣa-hīnaṁ
**cittaṁ** yasya tena **sūtena** tvayā hetunā \| **prāptaṁ** tvayā
**kilbiṣaṁ** pāpaṁ yena tasmāt \|\|29\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : sūtena** tvayā hetunā
**prāptaṁ kilbiṣaṁ** kalaṅko yena tasmāt \|\|29\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.30 \|\|**

**kiṁ nu vakṣye'bhisaṅgamya pitarau rāma-keśavau \|**

**dharmyād yuddhāt**[^17] **apakrāntaḥ pṛṣṭas tatrātmanaḥ kṣamam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : pitarau** **rāma-kṛṣṇāv
abhisaṅgamya** tat-pārśvaṁ gatvā tābhyāṁ **pṛṣṭaḥ** sva-yogyaṁ **kiṁ
nu** **vakṣyāmi** ? iti \|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : tatra** pitṛ-pārśve \| **kiṁ
vakṣyāmi** ? na kim api vaktuṁ yogyo bhaviṣyāmīty arthaḥ \|\|30\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** vairi-vadhādinā svān
ramayatīti **rāmaḥ**, **keśavaś** ca avahelayā mahā-daitya-keśi-sūdanāt,
tau iti tayor mahāvīryatvaṁ[^18] sūcitam \| **dharmyāt** puṇyajāt
śubhakarāt sva-dharma-yogyād vā ity avaśya-kṛtyatvam uktam \|
**apakrānto** bhaṅgaṁ prāptaḥ, **ātmano** me **kṣamaṁ** yogyaṁ karma
**kiṁ** katarad vakṣye ? api tu na kiñcid apīty arthaḥ \| yad vā, kṣamaṁ
hitaṁ sva-dharma-pālana-lakṣaṇaṁ **pṛṣṭaḥ** san \| evaṁ mama mahatī
lajjā jātā \|\|30\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** vairi-vadhādinā svān ramayati
iti **rāmaḥ** \| **keśavaś** ca helayā keśi-sūdanāt, tāv iti tayor
mahā-vīryatvaṁ sūcitam \| dharmādy-avaśya-kṛtyatvam uktam **ātmanaḥ**
**kṣamaṁ** yogyaṁ karma \|\|30\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : kṣamaṁ** yogyam \|\|30\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.31 \|\|**

**vyaktaṁ me kathayiṣyanti hasantyo bhrātṛ-jāmayaḥ \|**

**klaibyaṁ kathaṁ kathaṁ vīra tavānyaiḥ kathyatāṁ mṛdhe \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : bhrātṛ-jāmayo** bhrātṛ-bhāryāḥ
**vyaktaṁ** niścitaṁ mat-**klaibyaṁ** **kathayiṣyanti** \| tat kathanam
anukaroti---**kathaṁ katham** iti \|\|31\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** tāsāṁ kathanaṁ
tat-kathanam \|\|31-32\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** upahāsaś cātīvābhūd ity
āha---**vyaktam** iti niścitaṁ sphuṭaṁ vā **klaibyam** ity asya pareṇāpy
anvayaḥ \| **anyaiḥ** śatrubhiḥ kṛtvā **mṛdhe** yuddha-madhye **tava**
klaibyaṁ katham abhūt, tat tvayā kathyatām \| tatra vīpsā ca \|
**vīra**! he śūra ! iti copahāsād eva \| yad vā, anyair janaiḥ kathaṁ
kathyatām? api tu na kenāpi kathayitavyam iti mā lajjasva ity arthaḥ \|
anyat samānam \|\|31\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** evaṁ mama mahatī
loka-dharma-vicyutir jātā upahāsaś cātīvābhūd ity āha---**vyaktam** iti
manya ity arthaḥ \| **bhrātaro**\'tra jyeṣṭhāḥ pitṛvyādi-putrāḥ jñeyāḥ
\| **klaibyam** ity asya pareṇānvayaḥ \| **anyaiḥ** śatrubhir hetubhiḥ
\| **tava** dainyaṁ katham abhūt ? tat tvayā **kathyatāṁ** \| tatra
vīpsā ca \| he vīra ! iti copahāsātiśayāt \| yad vā, anyair janaiḥ
kathaṁ kathyatām ? api tu naikenāpi kathayitavyam iti mā lajjasva ity
arthaḥ \| tad idaṁ tu sārathi-bhartsanārtham evāropya proktam
marma-bhedakasyedṛśa-vākyasya tābhir ātmīyābhir avyaktatvāt \|\|31\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : bhrātṛ-jāmayo**
bhrātṛ-bhāryāḥ \| he **vīra** ! **anyaiḥ** saha **mṛdhe** **tava
klaibyaṁ kathaṁ katham abhūt** vismaye dvitvam \|\|31-32\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.32 \|\|**

**sārathir uvāca---**

**dharmaṁ vijānatāyuṣman kṛtam etan mayā vibho \|**

**sūtaḥ kṛcchra-gataṁ rakṣed rathinaṁ sārathiṁ rathī \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : vibho** ! he samartha ! **etad**
apasarpaṇam \| **dharmam** āha---**sūta** iti \|\|32\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** na mayā kila
klība-cittatayā tvam apavāhitaḥ, kintu sva-dharmāpekṣayaivety
āha---**dharmam** iti \| **āyuṣman** ! he nitya-vigraha ! iti \| he
**vibho** ! iti ca \| tvayi katham apy aniṣṭa-śaṅkā nāsty eveti bhāvaḥ
\| tathāpi **kṛtam** \| kutaḥ? **dharmaṁ** **vi**śeṣeṇa **jānatā**,
**kṛcchra-gataṁ** kaṣṭaṁ prāptaṁ **sārathiṁ** ca **rathī rakṣet**
\|\|32\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : āyuṣmann** iti nitya-yoge matup
\| he sarva-kāla-vyāpaka ! **vibho** ! he sarva-deśa-vyāpaka ! iti tvayi
katham apy aniṣṭa-śaṅkā nāsty eveti bhāvaḥ \| tathāpi **kṛtaṁ** \| kutaḥ
? **dharmaṁ** **vi**śeṣeṇa **jānatā** **kṛcchra-gataṁ** kaṣṭa-prāptaṁ
**sārathiṁ** ca **rathī rakṣet** \|\|32\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ),
viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

**\...**

**\|\| 10.76.33 \|\|**

**etad viditvā tu bhavān mayāpovāhito raṇāt \|**

**upasṛṣṭaḥ pareṇeti mūrcchito gadayā hataḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : apovāhito**'panītaḥ \|
**upasṛṣṭa** upasargaṁ pīḍāṁ prāpta iti kṛtvā \| yataḥ **pareṇa**
śatruṇā **gadayā hataḥ** san mūrcchito niḥsaṁjñatāṁ gato **bhavān** iti
\|\|33\|\|

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe daśama-skandhe uttarārdhe

śrīdhara-svāmi-viracitāyāṁ bhāvārtha-dīpikāyām

ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ \|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : etad** vacanam \|\|33\|\|

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe daśama-skandhottarārdhe

śrī-vaṁśīdhara-viracite bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe

ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ \|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :**

iti śrīnātha-cakravarti-pāda-viracitāyāṁ caitanya-mañjūṣāyāṁ

ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ \|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** sva-doṣaṁ parihartuṁ tad
eva draḍhayann ukta-poṣa-nyāyenāha---**etad** iti \| **tu** eva, etad
eva jñātvā, na tv anyathety arthaḥ \| **kṛcchra-gatatvam**
evābhivyañjayati---**upasṛṣṭa** iti \| anyat tair vyākhyātam \|

yad vā, **gadayā hato\'pi mūrcchitaḥ**, samucchritas tejo-vṛddhiṁ
prāptaḥ, mahā-vīratva-svabhāvāt \| ataḥ **pareṇa** parameśvareṇa
śrī-kṛṣṇena upasṛṣṭaḥ punar janita iti matvā kṣaṇaṁ viśrāmārthaṁ
**mayopovāhito**\'poḍhaḥ \|\|33\|\|

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe daśama-skandhe uttarārdhe

śrī-śrīla-sanātana-gosvāmi-pāda-kṛtāyāṁ śrī-bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇyāṁ

śrī-daśama-ṭippaṇyāṁ ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ \|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : etad** iti \| **pareṇopasṛṣṭo
gadayā hato mūrcchitaś** ca **etad viditvā** ity anvayaḥ\|
**apovāhita** ity asminn o-kāra-madhyatvam ārṣam \|\|33\|\|

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe daśama-skandhe

śrīmaj-jīva-gosvāmi-kṛta-vaiṣṇava-toṣiṇyāṁ

ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ \|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate daśama-skandhīye
śrīmaj-jīva-gosvāmi-kṛta-krama-sandarbhe ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ
\|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe daśama-skandhe

śrīmaj-jīva-gosvāmi-kṛta-bṛhat-krama-sandarbhe

ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ \|\|76\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : apovāhitaḥ** apanītaḥ
**upasṛṣṭaḥ** pīḍita ity arthaḥ \| yato **gadayā hato** bhavāṁs tadānīṁ
**mūrcchito\'bhūt** iti **jñātvaiva mayā apovāhitaḥ** \| tataś ca dhiṅ
mūḍha māṁ naiva tvam ajñāsīr iti pratyuktir jñeyā \|\|33\|\|

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakti-cetasām \|

ṣaṭsaptatitamo\'dhyāyo daśame\'jani saṅgataḥ \|\|76\|\|

**\...**

(10.77)

## atha sapta-saptatitamo\'dhyāyaḥ

### bhagavatā saubha-sahitasya śālvasya vināśaḥ \| 

**\|\| 10.77.1 \|\|**

**śrī-śuka uvāca---**

**sa tūpaspṛśya**[^19] **salilaṁ daṁśito dhṛta-kārmukaḥ \|**

**naya māṁ dyumataḥ pārśvaṁ vīrasyety āha sārathim \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

sapta-yuk-saptatitame nānā-māyā-vicakṣaṇaḥ \|

kṛṣṇenāgatya śālvas tu hataḥ saubhaṁ ca cūrṇitam \|\|

**daṁśitaḥ** sannaddhaḥ \|\|1\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** āgatya rājasūyāt \| **sa**
pradyumnaḥ \|\|1\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : tu**-śabdo bhinnopakrame
\|\| **daṁśita** ity anena prāg-avajñayā kavacādy-agrahaṇaṁ sūcayati \|
**dhṛtam** udyataṁ **kārmukaṁ** yena saḥ \| krodha-bhareṇa dūrata eva
śarair **dyumato** jighāṁsayā \| nanu duṣṭa-pārśve punar gamanam
ayogyaṁ, tad anyatra neyam ? tatrāha---**vīrasya** mat-pratiyodhasya \|
ata ādau tad-vadhārthaṁ tat-pārśve nayanam evocitam iti bhāvaḥ \|\|1\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : tu**-śabdo bhinnopakrame \|
**daṁśita** iti sal-lakṣaṇārthaṁ madhye sūtenottāraṇāt **dhṛtam**
udyataṁ **kārmukaṁ** yena sa iti paramotsāho darśitaḥ \| atas tatraiva
nayane hetum āha---**vīrasya** iti \|\|1\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

sapta-saptatitame harir indraprasthato nija-purīṁ samupetya \|

sālvam ātta-bahu-māyam arīn drāk saubha-saktam ariṇaiva jaghāna \|\|

**sa tv** iti \| sūtena sārathya-dharma-sāvadhānena tathā kṛtaṁ \|
**sa** pradyumnas **tu** kṣātra-dharma-pravīṇaḥ \|
raṇa-vicyuti-rūpa-pratyavāya-parihārārthaṁ **salilam upaspṛśya
daṁśitaḥ** dhṛta-kavacaḥ \|\|1\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.2 \|\|**

**vidhamantaṁ sva-sainyāni dyumantaṁ rukmiṇī-sutaḥ \|**

**pratihatya pratyavidhyān nārācair aṣṭabhiḥ smayan \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : vidhamantaṁ** kṣapayantam \|
pratihasya pratirudhya \|\|2\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** upasarga-vaśād
**dhamatir** atra nāśane, śatṛ-pratyayaḥ \|\|2\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : pratihatya**
**sva-sainya**-kṣapaṇa-pratighātaṁ kṛtvā \| pratihṛtyeti pāṭhe
pāṭhāntare tad-vidha-mardanaṁ pratyakṣaṁ nirasyety arthaḥ \| **prati**
pratirūpatayā pratyaṅga-vyāptyā **vāvidhyat** \| **nārācair**
bāṇa-viśeṣaiḥ **smayan** smayamānaḥ līlayety arthaḥ \| yad vā,
prauḍhimāviṣkurvan \|\|2\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : pratihatya** **sva-sainyaṁ**
rundhānaṁ taṁ tasmān nirudhya **pratyavidhyata**
tat-kṛta-vedha-pratiyogitayā\'vidhyat \| **nārācair** bāṇa-viśeṣaiḥ
**smayan** smayamāna iti vīra-svabhāvatvenotsāha eva jāto, na tu krodha
iti ślāghitam \|\|2\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : pratihatya** re re yāvat
sāmarthyaṁ praharety uktvā tad-astra-ghātānantaraṁ tasmai
pratyastra-ghātaṁ samarpyety arthaḥ \| **nārācaiḥ** śaraiḥ \|\|2\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.3 \|\|**

**caturbhiś caturo vāhān sūtam ekena cāhanat \|**

**dvābhyāṁ dhanuś ca ketuṁ ca śareṇānyena vai śiraḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** aṣṭānāṁ viniyogam
āha---**caturbhir** iti \|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** *aṣṭānāṁ* bāṇānāṁ
*viniyogaṁ* kṛtyam \|\|3-4\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : vai** api \| **śiro**\'pi
ca-kārair vai-śabdena ca tat-tad-dhanane yaugapadyaṁ bodhayati \|\|3\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : vai** samuccaye **śiro**\'pīty
arthaḥ \|\|3\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** aṣṭānāṁ viniyogam
āha---**caturbhir** ity-ādi \|\|3\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.4 \|\|**

**gada-sātyaki-sāmbādyā jaghnuḥ saubha-pater balam \|**

**petuḥ samudre saubheyāḥ sarve sañchinna-kandharāḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : saubheyāḥ** saubha-sthāḥ \|\|4\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** na ca kevalaṁ sa eva
sva-vikramaṁ darśayāmāsa, tena vivardhitotsāhā anye\'pi yadu-pravīrā ity
āha---**gada-** iti \| **ādya**-śabdāt pūrvoktāś cārudeṣṇādayaḥ \|
**sarve** prāyaśa ity arthaḥ \|\|4\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** na kevalaṁ sa eva
sva-vikramaṁ darśayāmāsa, tena vivardhitotsāhā anye\'pi yadu-vīrā ity
āha---**gada-** iti \| **sarve** prāyaśa ity arthaḥ \|\|4\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : saubheyāḥ** saubhasthāḥ
\|\|4\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.5 \|\|**

**evaṁ yadūnāṁ śālvānāṁ nighnatām itaretaram \|**

**yuddhaṁ tri-nava-rātraṁ tad abhūt tumulam ulbaṇam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** navānāṁ rātrīṇāṁ samāhāro
**navarātram**, trayāṇāṁ nava-rātrāṇāṁ samāhāras **tri-navarātram** \|
sapta-viṁśatim aho-rātrāṇīty arthaḥ \| **tumulam** ākulam \| **ulbaṇaṁ**
ghoram \|\|5\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : tad** yuddham \|\|5\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : tri-navaratraṁ**
saptaviṁśaty ahorātrāṇi vyāpyety arthaḥ \|\|5\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : tri-navarātraṁ** vyāpya
\|\|5\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** trayāṇāṁ nava-rātrāṇāṁ
samāhāras **triṇavarātram** saptaviṁśatim ahorātrāṇi vyāpyety arthaḥ
\|\|5-7\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.6-7 \|\|**

**indraprasthaṁ gataḥ kṛṣṇa āhūto dharma-sūnunā \|**

**rājasūye'tha nivṛtte śiśupāle ca saṁsthite \|\|**

**kuru-vṛddhān anujñāpya munīṁś ca sa-sutāṁ pṛthām \|**

**nimittāny atighorāṇi paśyan dvāravatīṁ yayau \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** para-matam
upanyasyati---**indraprasthaṁ** **gata** ity-ādinā \|\|6-7\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** *para-mataṁ*
vyāsetara-matam \| *upanyasyati* kathayati śukaḥ \|\|6-8\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** svayaṁ vakṣyamāṇasya
satyasya śrī-bhagavac-caritasya śrī-vaiśampāyanādy-uktena virodham
āśaṅkya tad dūyayitvā parihartum utthāpayati---**indra-** ity-ādinā
udyata \[bhā.pu. 10.77.29\] ity antena \| **āhūto** dūta-dvārā etac ca
sabhā-parvoktānusāreṇa śrī-bādarāyaṇi-mate ca śrī-nāradoktyā
śrīmad-uddhava-mantreṇa svayam eva gamanaṁ, tac ca prāg uktam eva \|
evam anyad api bahulaṁ viruddham agre\'py ūhyam \| tac ca yathā-sthānam
abhīvyañjayitavyam \| **dharma-sūnunā** iti śrī-yudhiṣṭhirasya
sad-dharma-paratvam abhipretam \| ata eva tad-āhvānenanākṛṣṭatvāt
**kṛṣṇa** iti \|\| athāgamanānantaraṁ sa-parikare rājasūye niṣpatre
**sutāḥ** śrī-yudhiṣṭhirādayas tat-sahitāṁ **nimittāni** śakunāni sakhi
**paśyan** \|\|6-7\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : indra-** iti yugmakam \|
**āhūta** ivāhūtaḥ śrī-nārada-dvārā tādṛśa-vijñāpanāt **rājasūya**
ity-āder indraprastha-gamana-prayojane sarvasmin samāpta ity arthaḥ \|
atheti ceti vā pāṭhaḥ \| **nimittāni** pathi **paśyan** \|\|6-7\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ),
viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.8 \|\|**

**āha cāham ihāyāta ārya-miśrābhisaṅgataḥ \|**

**rājanyāś caidya-pakṣīyā nūnaṁ hanyuḥ purīṁ mama \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : āha ca** iti sva-gatam eva pathi
cintā-vijṛmbhita-bhāṣaṇam \| **ārya-miśrābhisaṅgato** balabhadra-sahitaḥ
\|\|8\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : iha** indraprasthe \|
**nūnaṁ** vitarke \|\|8\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : āryo** guruḥ śrī-balabhadraḥ \|
sa eva **miśraḥ** pūjyaḥ \| yad vā, āryeṇa tena miśrāḥ sahitā ye, tair
api **saṅgataḥ** \|\|8\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : āha ca** iti svagatam \|
**āryaḥ** śrī-balabhadraḥ, sa eva **miśraḥ** pūjyaḥ, tena
**abhisaṅgata** iti na śuka-mataṁ, kintu para-matam evoktaṁ,
tathaivopariṣṭād vyākhyāsyamānatvāt \|\|8\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.9 \|\|**

**vīkṣya tat kadanaṁ svānāṁ nirūpya pura-rakṣaṇam \|**

**saubhaṁ ca śālva-rājaṁ ca dārukaṁ prāha keśavaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** durnimitta-darśanākula-citta
evaṁ cintayan dvārakām āgatya svānāṁ **kadanaṁ vīkṣya, saubhaṁ ca
śālva-rājaṁ ca** vīkṣya, rāmaṁ **pura-rakṣaṇaṁ** prati **nirūpya**
niyujya **dārukaṁ** **prāha** ity anvayaḥ \|\|9\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : tac** chālva-kṛtam \|
**kadanaṁ** mardam, kadanaṁ marda-pāpayoḥ iti

medinī \|\|9\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** prakarṣeṇa
nyāya-pradarśanādina praṇayena vā āha \| yataḥ **keśavaḥ** sākṣāt
parameśvaraḥ, tat-svāmī vai eva \|\|9\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : vīkṣya** iti \| ṭīkāyāṁ
durnimittety-ādikam āgatyety antam adhyāhṛtam \|\|9\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** evaṁ vicintayann eva
dvārakām āgatya \| tatra ca śālva-prāpitaṁ **svānāṁ kadanaṁ vīkṣya**
**purāṇām** antaḥ-pura-sthānāṁ śrī-rukmiṇy-ādīnāṁ **rakṣaṇaṁ nirūpya**
tāḥ sarvāḥ paṭṭamahiṣīḥ senānī-dvārā gupta-mārgeṇa dvārakā-vāsa-madhyaṁ
ca praveśyety arthaḥ \| **śālva-rājaṁ** ca vīkṣya \|\|9\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.10 \|\|**

**rathaṁ prāpaya me sūta śālvasyāntikam āśu vai \|**

**sambhramas te na kartavyo māyāvī saubha-rāḍ ayam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : te** tvayā \|\|10\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : sambhramo** bhayam,
sambhramaḥ sādhvase\'pi syāt saṁvegādarayor api iti medinī \|\|10-12\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : āśv** eva \| **māyāvī** iti
**sambhramaḥ** sādhvasam \| yad vā, **sambhramo na kartavyaḥ**
vyākula-cittena na bhāvyaṁ, kintu sāvadhānenaivety arthaḥ \| yato\'yaṁ
śālvo māyāvī tatra hetuḥ---saubhena mayamāyāmayayānena rājata iti tathā
saḥ \| yad vā, svato māyāvī punaś ca **saubharāṭ** saubha-ratiḥ
\|\|10\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : vai** eva \| **āśv** eva
**sambhramaḥ** sādhvasānubhāvaḥ āvego **na kartavyaḥ** \| yato
**māyāvī**, na tu svato vīraḥ \| **saubhena** ca māyāmayenaiva rājñā iti
tathā \|\|10\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ),
viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.11 \|\|**

**ity uktaś codayāmāsa ratham āsthāya dārukaḥ \|**

**viśantaṁ dadṛśuḥ sarve sve pare cāruṇānujam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : āsthāya** samyag adhiṣṭhāya
**aruṇānujaṁ** dhvaje vartamānaṁ garuḍam \|\|11\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : viśantaṁ** purīṁ
yuddha-sthalaṁ vā praviśantaṁ dūrād eva **dadṛśuḥ** \| ratha-dhvajopari
vartamānatvāt \| **sve** yādavāḥ **pare** śālvādayaḥ \|\|11\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : viśantaṁ** yuddham iti śeṣaḥ
\|\|11\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tataś ca **aruṇānujaṁ**
dhvaje pravartamānaṁ śrī-garuḍam \|\|11\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.12 \|\|**

**śālvaś ca kṛṣṇam ālokya hata-prāya-baleśvaraḥ**[^20] **\|**

**prāharat kṛṣṇa-sūtāya śaktiṁ bhīma-ravāṁ mṛdhe \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : hata-prāyasya balasya** sainyasya
**īśvaraḥ** \|\|12\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ), śrīnātha-cakravartī
(caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : ca** tu \| **śālvas** tv
iti śrī-garuḍa-darśanena yādavānāṁ paramānande jāte\'pi tatraiva
duṣṭasya tasya krodhādy-utpādakatayā bhinnopakramāt kṛṣṇaṁ
sva-sakha-śiśupālādīnāṁ prāṇākarṣakam iti bhāvaḥ \|
**hata-prāya-baleśvaro**\'pi **mṛdhe prāharat** cikṣepa \|\|12\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** hata-prāya-baleśvaro\'pi
**mṛdhe prāharat** prahārthaṁ cikṣepa \|\|12\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : hata-prāyāḥ baleśvarāḥ**
senānyo yaḥ saḥ \|\|12-13\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.13 \|\|**

**tām āpatantīṁ nabhasi maholkām iva raṁhasā \|**

**bhāsayantīṁ diśaḥ śauriḥ sāyakaiḥ śatadhācchinat \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : tāṁ** śaktim \|\|13\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : raṁhasā** vegena **nabhasy
āpatantīṁ** **maholkām** iveti raṁhasā patane diśāṁ bhāsane ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ
\| **nabhasy evācchinad** iti vā \| yataḥ **śaurir**
nijāśeṣaiśvarya-prakaṭanārthaṁ śūrya-vaṁśe\'vatīrṇaḥ sākṣād bhagavān
\|\|13\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : nabhasy āpatantīṁ** nabhasy eva
**acchinad** ity arthaḥ \|\|13\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ),
viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.14 \|\|**

**taṁ ca ṣoḍaśabhir viddhvā bāṇaiḥ saubhaṁ ca khe bhramat \|**

**avidhyac chara-sandohaiḥ khaṁ sūrya iva raśmibhiḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : taṁ ca** śālvam \|
**śara-sandohaiḥ** śara-jālaiḥ \| **khaṁ sūrya iva raśmibhir** iti
sunīlatva-vipulatvādibhir ākāśopamā saubhasya \|
acintya-vega-bāhulyādibhiḥ śarāṇāṁ raśmi-sādṛśyam \| ayatnenaiva
raśmi-vac chara-jāla-prasāraṇāt sūrya-tulyaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa iti \|\|14\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : taṁ** śālvam \|\|14\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī), jīva-gosvāmī
(laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : khe bhramad** api \|\|14\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : khaṁ sūrya iva** iti
saubhasya śyāmatva-tvaritatvābhyām ākāśena upamā śarāṇām
asaṅkhyatva-tāpakatvābhyāṁ raśmibhiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarva-tejaḥ-parābhāvakatayā
sūryeṇa \|\|14\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.15-16 \|\|**

**śālvaḥ śaures tu doḥ savyaṁ sa-śārṅgaṁ śārṅga-dhanvanaḥ \|**

**bibheda nyapatad dhastāc chārṅgam āsīt tad adbhutam \|\|**

**hāhā-kāro mahān āsīd bhūtānāṁ tatra paśyatām \|**

**ninadya saubha-rāḍ uccair idam āha janārdanam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : dor** bāhum \|\|15-16\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : tac** chārṅga-patanam
\|\|15\|\| **tatra** yuddhe \| **idaṁ** vakṣyamāṇam \|\|16\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** agre sa-nyāyam
atidūṣayituṁ sarvathā viruddhaṁ para-matam upahasann ivāha---**sālva**
ity-ādinā \| **śārṅgadhanvano**\'pi etad ativiruddham eva \|
saccidānanda-ghana-vigrahasya bhedanāsambhavāt sarasvatī-stuter atra
vāstavo\'rtho vartamāno\'pi na vyākhyeyaḥ, para-matasya duṣṭatvāt \| ata
eva tair api na sūcitaḥ \| **janānāṁ** tādṛśānāṁ duṣṭānām **ardanam**
apy **āha** iti dhṛṣṭatā nirbuddhitā sūcitā \|\|15-16\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** doṣo napuṁsakatvaṁ ca dṛśyate
\| savyaṁ dor acchinat tasya iti raghu-kāvyāc **chārṅgadhanvano**\'pi
\|\|15\|\| **janānāṁ** tādṛśānāṁ duṣṭānām **ardanam** api līlayaiva
tādṛśatām anukurvantaṁ tam **āha** iti dhṛṣṭatā nirbuddhitā ca sūcitā
\|\|16\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sālva ity-ādi
śloka-dvayaṁ na śuka-sammatam \| doḥ savyam iti doṣo napuṁsakatvam api
dṛśyate \| savyaṁ dor acchinat tasya iti raghu-kāvyāt **tat**
śārṅga-patanam **adbhutaṁ** tad-bhuja-balasya aparimeyatvāt
\|\|15-17\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.17 \|\|**

**yat tvayā mūḍha naḥ sakhyur bhrātur bhāryā hṛtekṣatām \|**

**pramattaḥ sa sabhā-madhye tvayā vyāpāditaḥ sakhā \|\|**

**taṁ tvādya niśitair bāṇair aparājita-māninam \|**

**nayāmy apunar-āvṛttiṁ yadi tiṣṭher mamāgrataḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : sakhyuḥ** śiśupālasya \|
**īkṣatām** asmākam \| **pramatto**'navahitaḥ \| **vyāpādito** nihataḥ
\|\|17\|\| **aparājito**'ham iti **māninaṁ** mānavantam \|
**apunar-āvṛttiṁ** mṛtyum \| **tiṣṭheḥ** sthāsyasi \|\|18\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** sakhitvād eva **bhrātur**
ity uktam \| **sa** śiśupālaḥ \|\|17\|\| **taṁ** sakhi-hantāram
\|\|18\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** sakhitvād evāsmākaṁ
**bhrātuḥ** sva-paitṛṣvaseyasya vā **sabhā-madhye**, na tu yuddha-madhye
ataḥ **pramatto**\'navahitaḥ, ata eva **vyāpāditaḥ** \| anyathā
**tvayā**\'sau hantuṁ na yogya iti bhāvaḥ \| **tvayā** iti punaruktyā
vyāpādanasya tad-eka-kartṛkatvena parama-dveṣyatvaṁ tathā **sakhā** iti
cāntaḥ-śoka-viśeṣaṁ mitrārtham avaśya-pratikṛtyaṁ ca sūcayati \|\|17\|\|
**yadi** ity adhunaiva mad-bhayāt kila palāyiṣyasa iti bhāvaḥ \|\|18\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : yad** iti yugmakam \| **yat**
yena **tvayā** asmākaṁ sakhyus tava tu **bhrātuḥ** paitṛṣvaseyasya
**sabhā-madhye,** na tu yuddha-madhye, ataḥ **pramattaḥ** anavahitaḥ,
ata eva **vyāpāditaḥ** \| punaruktyā vyāpādanasya tad-eka-kartṛtvena
parama-dveṣyatvaṁ tathā **sakhā** iti cāntaḥ-śoka-viśeṣaṁ, sakhā iti
mitrārtha-kṛtyasya avaśyakatvaṁ ca sūcayati---yadīty adhunaiva
mad-bhayāt kila palāyiṣyasa iti bhāvaḥ \|

gīr-devī-mate---\"amūḍha ! he parama-vidvan! asmākaṁ sakhyur bhrātuś ca
śiśupālasya tathā no\'smākaṁ ca īkṣatām īkṣamāṇānāṁ taṁ cāsmāṁś
cānādṛtyety arthaḥ \| yena **tvayā** bhāryā lakṣmītvān nijā jāyaiva
hṛtā, tathā pramattaḥ pītam adyādivan nānā-durvacanādy-unmatta-ceṣṭaḥ
so\'smat-sakhā vyāpāditaḥ\" \|\|17\|\|

**taṁ** na vidyate punar-āvṛttis tathā-bhūtaṁ tathā **aparājitaḥ**
kenāpy anabhibhūto **mānaḥ** pūjā tadvat taṁ ca tvāṁ tvadīyair eva
niśiter bāṇair hetubhir nayāmi gacchāmi praviśāmīty arthaḥ \| naya paya
gatau kintu mad-bhāgyam eva tatra sādhakatamam ity āha---yadīti
\|\|18\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he **mūḍha**!
**apunar-āvṛttiṁ** mṛtyuṁ **nayāmi** prāpayāmi \| bhāratī-pakṣe na
bhavati\| mūḍho yasmāt tathā-bhūta! na **sakhyuḥ bhrātus**
tvat-paitṛṣvaseyasya śiśupālasya **īkṣamāṇānām** asmākaṁ cety anādare
ṣaṣṭhī **bhāryā** lakṣmītvāt sva-strī **hṛtā** gṛhītā **niśitair bāṇaiḥ
aparājitaś** cāsau **mānī** ādara-pātraś ca, tam **apunar-āvṛttiṁ**
mokṣaṁ **nayāmi** nāyayāmīty arthaḥ \| yad vā, na bhavati punar-āvṛttiḥ
saṁsāro yasmāt, taṁ mokṣa-dāyinaṁ tvāṁ nayāmi prāpnomīty arthaḥ
\|\|18-20\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.19 \|\|**

**śrī-bhagavān uvāca---**

**vṛthā tvaṁ katthase manda na paśyasy antike'ntakam \|**

**pauruṣaṁ darśayanti sma śūrā na bahu-bhāṣiṇaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : antakaṁ** tavānta-kartāraṁ
mām ity arthaḥ \|\|19\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : katthase** ātmānaṁ
ślāghase, garveṇa bahu jalpasi vā \| tac ca yuktam evety āha---**manda**
! he nirbuddhe! duṣṭeti vā \| mandatvam evāha---neti \| āsannaṁ
mṛtyutvād īdṛśaṁ katthanaṁ yuktam eveti bhāvaḥ \| śūro\'pi tvaṁ na khalu
bhavasīty āha---pauruṣam iti \| smeti prasiddham evaitad ity arthaḥ
\|\|19\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : katthase** ātmānaṁ ślāghase \|
tac ca yuktam ity āha---**manda** ! he nirbuddhe! mandatvam evāha---neti
\| āsanna-mṛtyutvād īdṛśaṁ katthanaṁ yuktam eveti bhāvaḥ \| śūro\'pi na
khalu bhavasīty āha---pauruṣam iti \| smeti prasiddham evaitad ity
arthaḥ \|\|19\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ),
viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

**\...**

**\|\| 10.77.20 \|\|**

**ity uktvā bhagavāñ chālvaṁ gadayā bhīma-vegayā \|**

**tatāḍa jatrau saṁrabdhaḥ sa cakampe vamann asṛk \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : sa** śālvaḥ \|\|20\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : bhagavān** sarva-śaktimān,
**bhīmo** bhayaṅkaro **vego** nipāto yasyās tayā **saṁrabdhaḥ** kruddhaḥ
san **tatāḍa** etad api mahā-viruddhaṁ tena tathā tādṛśa-tāḍanena sadya
eva maraṇa-sambhavāt **sa** śālvaḥ \|\|20\|\|

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : sa** sālvaḥ \|\|20\|\|
